| 1:04:20| his father serving in Burma during World War II, and whereas in 1974 Garrett Hannes decided to join the ranks| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=3860)|

| 1:09:50| Whereas Tom Jensen passed away on July 24, 2018, at the age of 83,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4190)|
| 1:09:56| and whereas Tom Jensen served 12 years in the Tennessee General Assembly| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4196)|
| 1:10:00| as State Representative for Knox County from 1966 to 1978,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4200)|
| 1:10:05| and served as Minority Leader for eight of those years,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4205)|
| 1:10:09| and whereas during his tenure as a member of the Tennessee General Assembly,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4209)|
| 1:10:13| Tom Jensen was a tireless supporter of funding for buildings and programs for the University of Tennessee,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4213)|
| 1:10:18| domestic violence protection programs, completion of the interstate system,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4218)|
| 1:10:23| education including raising of teachers' salaries, historical preservation, and support for the arts,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4223)|
| 1:10:29| and whereas recognizing the benefits of early childhood education,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4229)|
| 1:10:33| Tom Jensen considered the creation of a state kindergarten system| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4233)|
| 1:10:36| to be the most significant legislation he's helped to enact,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4236)|
| 1:10:40| and whereas Tom Jensen was the accessible public servant,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4240)|
| 1:10:44| and as such he initiated a downtown Saturday morning open legislative forum| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4244)|
| 1:10:49| where citizens could talk directly to their legislator when the General Assembly was in session,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4249)|
| 1:10:54| and whereas Tom Jensen served as President of the National Conference of State Legislators,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4254)|
| 1:10:59| representing the nation's 8,000 state legislators,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4259)|
| 1:11:02| and in that role he was frequent speaker for the other state legislators,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4262)|
| 1:11:06| even meeting in the Oval Office to present the proposals of the NCSL to the President| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4266)|
| 1:11:12| and testifying before congressional committees about state legislative issues,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=4272)|

| 2:15:48| with an inventory of specialized equipment not available through any other Knox County agency,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=8148)|
| 2:15:54| KBRS responds to emergency calls countywide 24 hours a day, seven days a week.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=8154)|
| 2:16:00| We serve Knox County with specialized rescue teams in the areas of vehicle rescue, cave and vertical rescue,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=8160)|
| 2:16:07| high angle rescue, water rescue, confined space, trench collapse, structural collapse, and heavy rescue.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=8167)|
| 2:16:15| Our increased population and service provision expansion has triggered the cost to provide the level of service| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=8175)|
| 2:16:22| that Knox County has come to expect, obviously, to rise.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=8182)|

| 2:16:33| This is after expenses were addressed by closing two stations| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComR267180827?start=8193)|
